Illustrator Export Settings

To arrive at the slimmed-down 1kb version of this SVG, choose these options in Illustrator:

  1. File > Export > Export As...
  2. Choose filename/location
  3. Choose Format: SVG (svg)
  4. Click Export
  5. In the SVG Options pane choose:
    • Styling: Internal CSS
    • Font: SVG
    • Images: Preserve
    • Object IDs: Minimal
    • Decimal: 2
    • Check Minify
    • Check Responsive
  6. Click Ok
